14/06/22, 11:11 - Harsh Indus: //copy file
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
int fcpy(FILE * sourceFile, FILE * destFile);

int main()
{
    FILE *sourceFile;
    FILE *destFile;
    char sourcePath[100];
    char destPath[100];

    int count;
    printf("Enter source file path: ");
    scanf("%s", sourcePath);
    printf("Enter destination file path: ");
    scanf("%s", destPath);


    sourceFile  = fopen(sourcePath, "r");
    destFile    = fopen(destPath,   "w");


    if (sourceFile == NULL || destFile == NULL)
    {

        printf("\nUnable to open file.\n");
        printf("Please check if file exists and you have read/write privilege.\n");

        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
    }

    count = fcpy(sourceFile, destFile);
    printf("\nFiles copied successfully.\n");
    printf("%d characters copied.\n", count);

    fclose(sourceFile);
    fclose(destFile);

    return 0;
}

int fcpy(FILE * sourceFile, FILE * destFile)
{
    int  count = 0;
    char ch;

    /* Copy file contents character by character. */
    while ((ch = fgetc(sourceFile)) != EOF)
    {
        fputc(ch, destFile);

        /* Increment character copied count */
        count++;
    }

    return count;
}

17/08/22, 19:06 - Het Indus CR: General Instructions for Gokulashtami Celebration: 

 

This celebration is a small step to cherish our culture and traditions. The event entails the relevance of Indian ethos, which is somehow felt fading among this generation. The purpose is to encourage students as they put their best talent forward.


Theme- To express gratitude to the lord Krishna, also to cherish and bring out the best in one another.

Dress code- Ethnic Wear


The activities planned: 

This is going to be an offline activity and where students have to register themselves and select their choice of activity out of the following options:

 

1. Dress up like Krishna and his acquaintance(Fancy Dress Competition)- Individual   Activity

This competition will bring festivities on the campus, wherein, students have to disguise themselves as lord Krishna or his acquaintance. Evaluation will be based on creativity as well as presentability. It is both an individual activity as well as a group activity, based on the theme.

 

2. Poster competition - This competition is based on creativity with the content as per the given theme (Krishna).

* This is an individual event.

* Students have to bring drawing sheets and poster colors (No other colors are allowed) and other necessary supplies on their own.

* The Time provided for the same is 60 minutes.

* Final decision will be on the overall outcome, and the jury will announce the same.

 

3. Curd Pot (Dahi Handi) :  The most significant event of the program was ‚Äú Dahi Handi‚Äù. It is a group activity, where the group leader has to register via the provided link. Kindly ensure your safety while indulging in the activity.


* Winners and Runner Ups will get the certificates.

 

** Registrations will be closed by the EOD(17/8/22).

 

 

Kindly check the Google form attached for more information and register yourself. We would love to see you all participate.

 

https://forms.gle/fNm4VFAXWzAjR8Sz6

16/02/23, 11:54 - Het Indus CR: package javaapplication1;

import java.util.Scanner;
class myexcept extends Exception
{
    myexcept()
    {
        
    }
    myexcept(String s1)
    {
        super(s1);
    }
    
}

public class myfirst {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        
        try
        { int a,b,c;
            System.out.println("enter a and b");
            Scanner sc= new Scanner(System.in);
            a=sc.nextInt();
            b=sc.nextInt();
            
            if(b==0)
            {
                throw  new myexcept(" b value mustnot be 0");
            }    
            c=a/b;
            System.out.println(" c="+c);
            
        }
        catch(myexcept e)
        {
            //e.printStackTrace();
            String mes= e.getMessage();
            System.out.println(" "+mes);
        }
        finally
        {
            System.out.println(" program execute sucessfully");
        }
    }
}
